'## Synopsis\n\n FIFA 23 is a football video game published by EA Sports. It is the 30th installment in the FIFA series that is developed by EA Sports, the final installment under the FIFA banner, and released worldwide on 30 September 2022 for Nintendo Switch, PlayStation 4, PlayStation 5, Windows, Xbox One, and Xbox Series X/S.\n\n ## Overview\n\n Kylian Mbappé and Sam Kerr are the cover athletes for the standard and legacy editions. Listed in Guinness World Records as the best-selling sports video game franchise in the world, the game is the final under the 29-year partnership between EA and FIFA. Future football games by EA are named under the banner of EA Sports FC (alternatively just EASFC EAFC or FC ).\n\n ## Gameplay\n\n ### Crossplay\n FIFA 23 features a degree of crossplay. Crossplay is available in FIFA Ultimate Team (FUT) Division Rivals (excluding co-op), FUT Champions, FUT Ultimate Online Draft, FUT Online Friendlies (excluding Co-Op), FUT Play a Friend, Online Friendlies, Online Seasons (excluding Co-Op Seasons) and the Virtual representation of the Bundesliga. However, crossplay is limited to consoles that fall within the same console generation. For example, those on the PlayStation 4 are able to play with and against players on Xbox One, but not the PlayStation 5 or Xbox Series X/S and vice versa. Pro Clubs will not support crossplay.\n\n The decision to omit Pro Clubs from crossplay has received criticism from the FIFA community. Furthermore, the option to delete Ultimate Team data has been removed due to most players not using that option, while an option to rename the club\s name outside of the Objectives screen has been added instead. In previous FIFA titles, players can only use the Delete Club option 4 times, as they are allowed to create a club 5 times.\n\n ### HyperMotion2 and Technical Dribbling\n The game features what\s being dubbed as HyperMotion2 a system of match capture with machine learning from real-life football matches to create over 6,000 in-game animations. Technical Dribbling uses what is being called the Active Touch system to improve the footballer\s path to the ball and improve a player\s turning and dribbling with more responsiveness. Both systems are exclusive to current-generation versions (i.e. PS5, Xbox Series X/S, and PC).\n\n ## Characters\n\n ### New Icons and Removed Icons\n FIFA 23 features three new icons to its ICON Collection with the addition of Gerd Müller, Xabi Alonso, and Jairzinho. With new additions to these three, 8 of the previously added icons are missing from the Icons List released by EA Sports. Diego Maradona, Ryan Giggs, Pep Guardiola, Deco, Marc Overmars, and Filippo Inzaghi have been removed as icons for FIFA 23. Jay-Jay Okocha and Hidetoshi Nakata have been removed as icons for FIFA 23 but are now featured as heroes.\n\n ### New Heroes\n FIFA 23, in an exclusive deal with Marvel, features 21 new heroes to the existing heroes collection from FIFA 22 with the additions of: Lúcio, Jean-Pierre Papin, Rudi Völler, Diego Forlán, Rafael Márquez, Javier Mascherano, Ricardo Carvalho, Tomas Brolin, Harry Kewell, Yaya Touré, Claudio Marchisio, Landon Donovan, Joan Capdevila, Sidney Govou, Dirk Kuyt, Park Ji-sung, Włodzimierz Smolarek, Saeed Al-Owairan, and Peter Crouch, with the late addition of Ledley King after the game\s release.\n\n ## World Cup Game Modes\n\n FIFA 23 features the men\s World Cup game mode and the women\s World Cup game mode, replicating the 2022 FIFA World Cup and the 2023 FIFA Women\s World Cup. This is the only title in the series to feature both World Cups as special modes.\n\n ## Women\s Club Football\n\n This entry in the FIFA video game series is the first to introduce women\s club football. England\s FA Women\s Super League and the French Division 1 Féminine are included at launch, with more women\s football leagues planned to be added later on. This comes alongside Sam Kerr, who plays for Chelsea Women, becoming the first female footballer to feature on the global front cover of the game. On 18 October 2022, EA Sports announced the inclusion of the UEFA Women\s Champions League in the game for early 2023. On 6 March 2023, EA announced the addition of the UEFA Women\s Champions League and the National Women\s Soccer League beginning on 15 March 2023. On 14 March, EA announced the UWCL and NWSL update would be available by 23 March due to issues encountered during testing.\n\n ## Licences\n\n FIFA 23 contains over 30 licensed leagues, over 100 licensed stadiums, over 700 clubs, and more than 19,000 players. Roma, Atalanta, Lazio, and Napoli are not featured in FIFA 23 due to their exclusivity agreements with rival game eFootball and are instead known as Roma FC, Bergamo Calcio, Latium, and Napoli FC respectively. The game retains the players\ likenesses, but the official badge, kits, and stadiums are replaced with custom designs and generic stadiums created by EA Sports. Juventus, having been similarly absent for the past three entries and thus known as Piemonte Calcio, are featured in the game, however.\n\n The game no longer features the teams of the J1 League, due to EA and J.League\s six-year partnership coming to an end. Almost all Latin American leagues were also removed from the game, with only the Argentine Primera División remaining, the teams that contend the Copa Libertadores and Copa Sudamericana are also still present. The Russian Premier League remained absent from the game as well, due to the ongoing Russian invasion of Ukraine.\n\n New stadiums added to the game include the Philips Stadion, home of PSV Eindhoven, the Europa-Park Stadion, home of SC Freiburg, the Banc of California Stadium, home of Los Angeles FC, and the Academy Stadium, home of Manchester City Women. The Juventus Stadium, home of Juventus, is also added, having been absent from the past few entries due to license issues. Nottingham Forest\s home ground, the City Ground, was added post-launch via an update, thus ensuring all 20 Premier League clubs have their respective stadiums. Bayern Munich and Barcelona are also featured in the game with licensed players and kits but do not have their stadium licenses and thus play in generic stadiums.\n\n The game features fictional club AFC Richmond and their stadium Nelson Road from the Apple TV+ series Ted Lasso.\n\n ## Soundtrack\n\n Alongside the game\s main soundtrack, 40 of the 100 popular tracks from previous FIFA titles — collectively known as the Ultimate FIFA Soundtrack — were added to the game in November 2022. These songs included Song 2 by Blur (FIFA: Road to World Cup 98), Love Me Again by John Newman (FIFA 14), and The Nights by Avicii (FIFA 15). As a result of these additions, FIFA 23\s soundtrack is the largest in the series.\n'	,

'## Synopsis\n\n Embark on an epic journey of fantasy and adventure with Final Fantasy XVI, the latest installment in the iconic role-playing game series. Set in a world of swords and sorcery, players are thrust into a sprawling narrative of political intrigue, magical warfare, and ancient prophecies as they navigate the tumultuous kingdom of Valisthea. With its richly detailed world, complex characters, and gripping storyline, Final Fantasy XVI invites players to embark on a quest of heroism and sacrifice as they uncover the secrets of the mystical Mothercrystals and confront the dark forces that threaten to plunge the realm into chaos. With its dynamic combat system, breathtaking visuals, and emotionally resonant storytelling, Final Fantasy XVI offers an immersive and unforgettable RPG experience that captures the essence of the legendary franchise while introducing new twists and innovations to delight both longtime fans and newcomers alike.\n\n ## Gameplay\n\n Final Fantasy XVI is an MMORPG, featuring a persistent world where players can interact with each other and the environment. Players create and customize their characters for use in the game, including name, race, gender, facial features, and starting class. Unlike in the original release, players may only choose to be a Disciple of War or Magic as a starting class—Disciples of the Hand and Land are initially unavailable. Players must also select a game server for each character. While all supported languages are available on every server, data centers are located in specific regions (i.e., North America, Europe, Japan, and Oceania) to reduce latency between client and server, and players are advised to choose a server in their region. Regardless of server or language, players can use a large library of automatically translated game terms and general phrases, allowing players who speak different languages to communicate.\n\n ## Interface\n\n PC and home console versions use a unified user interface and control scheme. Any combination of a keyboard, mouse, and game controller may be used, for console players, wireless or USB keyboard and mouse are required for the former. On PC and macOS, the game defaults to drag and drop windows, while on the console versions of XIV, the default interface resembles the PlayStation 3\s XrossMediaBar. This bar is used to access all menus, maps, logs, and configuration options. The head-up display for both versions includes a message log, party status menu, mini-map, and action bar. The UI offers extensive customization options.\n\n ## Character Progression\n\n Players improve their characters by gaining experience points (EXP) and acquiring stronger equipment. After gaining enough XP, the character will level up improving their statistics, enhancing the character\s performance and often learning new actions. Primary sources of experience points in Final Fantasy XIV include completing quests, exploring instanced dungeons, participating in Full Active Time Events (FATEs), and slaying monsters in the world. Quests, including the main scenario questline, are generally short, specific tasks given to the player by non-player characters which reward items and EXP. Completing main scenario quests progresses the overarching plot of the game. Some quests are repeatable, either daily quests repeatable each day, or Levequests which consume leve allowances that the player slowly accrues over time. Dungeons often require multiple players to form a party to enter, but the Duty Support system enables the player to play certain dungeons alone, supported by computer-controlled party members. Some dungeons are for lower-leveled players to gain EXP quickly while others are for experienced players to collect rare items, equipment, and currency. The Duty Roulette system randomly assigns the player to an accessible dungeon, and once per day, awards additional bonus EXP scaled to character level on completion. FATEs permit large groups of players, whether or not they are in a party, to participate in a shared task in the world. These location-specific events include battles with notorious monsters, defending locations, escorting non-player characters, culling wildlife, and assaulting enemy fortresses, among other types. Finally, each enemy the player kills provides EXP, with further EXP available from the Hunting Log, for killing a fixed amount of specific creatures. At maximum level, character progression focuses entirely on acquiring stronger equipment, raising the character\s item level . This equipment can be gained through a variety of sources including endgame dungeons, crafting, raids, primal battles, and elite mark hunts.\n\n'	,	
'## Sinopsis\n\n Embárcate en un viaje épico de fantasía y aventura con *Final Fantasy XVI*, la última entrega en la icónica serie de juegos de rol. Ambientado en un mundo de espadas y hechicería, los jugadores son lanzados a una narrativa expansiva de intriga política, guerra mágica y antiguas profecías mientras navegan por el tumultuoso reino de Valisthea. Con su mundo ricamente detallado, personajes complejos y una historia cautivadora, *Final Fantasy XVI* invita a los jugadores a embarcarse en una búsqueda de heroísmo y sacrificio mientras descubren los secretos de los místicos Cristales Madre y enfrentan a las fuerzas oscuras que amenazan con sumir al reino en el caos. Los jugadores crean y personalizan sus personajes para usar en el juego, incluyendo nombre, raza, género, rasgos faciales y clase inicial. A diferencia del lanzamiento original, los jugadores solo pueden elegir ser Discípulos de la Guerra o de la Magia como clase inicial, los Discípulos de la Mano y la Tierra no están disponibles inicialmente. Los jugadores también deben seleccionar un servidor de juego para cada personaje. Aunque todos los idiomas admitidos están disponibles en cada servidor, los centros de datos están ubicados en regiones específicas (es decir, América del Norte, Europa, Japón y Oceanía) para reducir la latencia entre el cliente y el servidor, y se recomienda a los jugadores elegir un servidor en su región. Independientemente del servidor o idioma, los jugadores pueden usar una amplia biblioteca de términos de juego y frases generales traducidos automáticamente, lo que permite que los jugadores que hablan diferentes idiomas se comuniquen.\n\n ## Interfaz\n\n Las versiones de PC y consola doméstica utilizan una interfaz de usuario y un esquema de control unificados. Se puede usar cualquier combinación de teclado, ratón y mando de juego, para los jugadores de consola, se requieren teclado y ratón inalámbricos o USB para lo primero. En PC y macOS, el juego se ajusta a arrastrar y soltar ventanas, mientras que en las versiones de consola de XIV, la interfaz predeterminada se asemeja a la barra XrossMediaBar de PlayStation 3. Esta barra se utiliza para acceder a todos los menús, mapas, registros y opciones de configuración. La pantalla de visualización para ambas versiones incluye un registro de mensajes, un menú de estado del grupo, un mini mapa y una barra de acciones. La interfaz ofrece amplias opciones de personalización.\n\n ## Progresión de Personajes\n\n Los jugadores mejoran sus personajes obteniendo puntos de experiencia (EXP) y adquiriendo equipo más fuerte. Después de obtener suficientes XP, el personaje subirá de nivel mejorando sus estadísticas, mejorando el rendimiento del personaje y a menudo aprendiendo nuevas acciones. Las principales fuentes de puntos de experiencia en *Final Fantasy XIV* incluyen completar misiones, explorar mazmorras instanciadas, participar en Eventos de Tiempo Activo Completo (FATE), y matar monstruos en el mundo. Las misiones, incluida la línea de misiones escenario principal son generalmente tareas cortas y específicas que el jugador recibe de personajes no jugadores y que recompensan objetos y EXP. Completar misiones del escenario principal progresa en la trama general del juego. Algunas misiones son repetibles, ya sea misiones diarias repetibles cada día, o Levequests que consumen leve allowances que el jugador acumula lentamente con el tiempo. Las mazmorras a menudo requieren que varios jugadores formen un grupo para entrar, pero el sistema Duty Support permite que el jugador juegue ciertas mazmorras solo, con el apoyo de miembros del grupo controlados por la computadora. Algunas mazmorras son para jugadores de nivel bajo para ganar EXP rápidamente, mientras que otras son para jugadores experimentados para recolectar objetos raros, equipo y moneda. El sistema Duty Roulette asigna al jugador aleatoriamente a una mazmorra accesible, y una vez al día, otorga EXP adicional de bonificación escalada al nivel del personaje al completarse. Los FATE permiten que grupos grandes de jugadores, estén o no en un grupo, participen en una tarea compartida en el mundo. Estos eventos específicos de la ubicación incluyen batallas con monstruos notorios, defensa de ubicaciones, escolta de personajes no jugadores, exterminio de vida silvestre y asalto a fortalezas enemigas, entre otros tipos. Finalmente, cada enemigo que el jugador mate proporciona EXP, con EXP adicional disponible en el Registro de Caza, para matar una cantidad fija de criaturas específicas. En el nivel máximo, la progresión del personaje se centra únicamente en adquirir un equipo más fuerte, aumentando el nivel de objeto del personaje. Este equipo se puede obtener a través de una variedad de fuentes, incluidas mazmorras de juego final, elaboración, incursiones, batallas primigenias y cacerías de marcas de élite.\n',

'## Synopsis\n\n Step into the high-stakes world of tactical shooter esports with *Valorant*, a thrilling multiplayer game that combines precise gunplay with unique character abilities. Set in a near-future Earth where elite operatives known as Agents battle it out in intense 5v5 matches, *Valorant* offers a dynamic and strategic gameplay experience unlike any other. Players choose from a diverse roster of Agents, each with their own distinct abilities and playstyles, as they compete in a variety of game modes, including Bomb Defusal and Spike Rush. With its emphasis on teamwork, communication, and skillful gunplay, *Valorant* challenges players to outmaneuver and outsmart their opponents in fast-paced, round-based matches. From tense tactical showdowns and clutch plays to pulse-pounding firefights and explosive abilities, *Valorant* delivers an adrenaline-fueled gaming experience that keeps players on the edge of their seats. \n\n ## Details\n\n *Valorant* is a free-to-play first-person tactical hero shooter developed and published by Riot Games, for Windows. Teased under the codename Project A in October 2019, the game began a closed beta period with limited access on April 7, 2020, followed by a release on June 2, 2020. The development of the game started in 2014. *Valorant* takes inspiration from the Counter-Strike series, borrowing several mechanics such as the buy menu, spray patterns, and inaccuracy while moving.\n\n ## Gameplay\n\n *Valorant* is a team-based first-person tactical hero shooter set in the near future. Players play as one of a set of Agents, characters based on several countries and cultures around the world. In the main game mode, players are assigned to either the attacking or defending team with each team having five players on it. Agents have unique abilities, each requiring charges, as well as a unique ultimate ability that requires charging through kills, deaths, orbs, or objectives. Every player starts each round with a classic pistol and one or more signature ability charges. Other weapons and ability charges can be purchased using an in-game economic system that awards money based on the outcome of the previous round, any kills the player is responsible for, and any objectives completed. The game has an assortment of weapons including secondary guns like sidearms and primary guns like submachine guns, shotguns, machine guns, assault rifles and sniper rifles.\n\n ### Game Modes\n\n - **Unrated**: In the standard non-ranked mode, the match is played as best of 25 - the first team to win 13 rounds wins the match. The attacking team has a bomb-type device called the Spike, which they must deliver and activate on one of the multiple specified locations (bomb sites).\n - **Spike Rush**: A mode where the match is played as best of 7 rounds - the first team to win 4 rounds wins the match. Players begin the round with all abilities fully charged except their ultimate.\n - **Swiftplay**: A shortened version of the Unrated game mode, played as best of 9 rounds.\n - **Competitive**: Similar to Unrated matches with the addition of a win-based ranking system.\n - **Premier**: A path-to-pro competitive game mode aimed towards professional players.\n - **Deathmatch**: A free-for-all mode where players aim to reach a certain number of kills within a time limit.\n - **Team Deathmatch**: A team-based mode where the first team to reach a certain number of kills wins.\n - **Escalation**: A team-based mode where players progress through a series of weapons.\n - **Replication**: A mode where the entire team plays as the same agent.\n - **Snowball Fight**: A limited-time Team Deathmatch mode available during Christmas season.\n\n ### Agents\n\n Agents are divided into 4 roles: Duelists, Sentinels, Initiators, and Controllers, each with a different playstyle and abilities.\n\n - **Duelists**: Self-sufficient fraggers who specialize in attacking and entering bomb sites.\n - **Sentinels**: Defensive agents who lock down sites and protect teammates.\n - **Initiators**: Offensive agents who specialize in breaking through defensive positions.\n - **Controllers**: Agents who control territory and set up their team for success with smokes and crowd control.\n\n'	,

It released in early access in October 2023 and gained popularity on the Steam storefront.\n\n ## Gameplay\n\n *Lethal Company* is a cooperative video game for up to four players played in first-person perspective. Set in a retrofuturistic setting, players work as contracted employees of The Company . They are able to communicate with each other through the in-game proximity chat, as well as proximity text chat. Players are tasked with visiting abandoned moons in order to collect as much scrap as possible. Each moon has one facility containing procedurally-generated rooms, alongside valuable scrap, hazardous traps, and malicious creatures. Players must work quickly and return to their ship before midnight, or the autopilot will leave without them. If there are no living players on board the ship as it leaves the planet, all collected scrap will be lost. \n\n Collected scrap is sold at the Company moon, 71-Gordion, to obtain Company credits. At the end of each deadline, if the players sell enough scrap to reach the required quota, they will begin another three-day cycle with a higher profit goal. Failure to meet the Company\s quota results in players being ejected into space, this constitutes a game-over.\n\n The game offers nine playable moons, including the Company\s moon where collected scrap is sold. Moons differ in which and how many monsters spawn, as well as the amount and value of scrap available. Players must spend credits to access the most dangerous and lucrative moons. Moons may randomly have dangerous weather conditions, such as flooding or solar eclipses, that hinder players\ progress.\n\n Players will encounter a variety of creatures while exploring. Most are found inside each moon\s facility, but some will spawn outdoors. Most entities are hostile towards the players, though some creatures, like the Spore Lizard and Hoarding Bug, will remain passive until provoked. The game\s monsters include the Thumper, a two-legged beast that can reach high speeds but is bad at making tight turns, and the Bracken, a humanoid creature that stalks its prey before snapping its neck, but runs away when spotted. One of the most dangerous enemies is the Jester, an invincible creature inside a giant jack-in-the-box. It wanders harmlessly until it spots a player and starts turning their jack-in-the-box crank. After popping open, it will hunt and kill all players in the facility.\n'	,

('Minecraft',	'Minecraft',	2011	,'https://www.minecraft.net/es-es/minecraft-tips-for-beginners',	
'## Synopsis\n\n Dive into a boundless world of creativity and adventure with *Minecraft*, the iconic sandbox game that allows players to build, explore, and survive in procedurally generated worlds of endless possibility. Set in a blocky, pixelated universe where the only limit is your imagination, *Minecraft* offers players the freedom to shape their own destinies as they mine resources, craft tools, and construct elaborate structures from the ground up. From humble beginnings as a lone survivor in a vast wilderness to the heights of towering cities and sprawling civilizations, players embark on a journey of discovery and creation unlike any other. With its infinite landscapes, diverse biomes, and limitless opportunities for exploration and collaboration, *Minecraft* invites players of all ages to unleash their creativity and embark on epic adventures in a world limited only by their imagination. \n\n ## Details\n\n *Minecraft* is a 2011 sandbox game developed by Mojang Studios and originally released in 2009. The game was created by Markus Notch Persson in the Java programming language. Following several early private testing versions, it was first made public in May 2009 before being fully released on November 18, 2011, with Notch stepping down and Jens Jeb Bergensten taking over development. *Minecraft* has become the best-selling video game in history, with over 300 million copies sold and nearly 140 million monthly active players as of 2023. It has been ported to several platforms.\n\n ## Gameplay\n\n ### Overview\n *Minecraft* is a 3D sandbox game that has no required goals to accomplish, allowing players a large amount of freedom in choosing how to play the game. However, there is an achievement system, known as advancements in the Java Edition of the game, trophies on the PlayStation ports, and achievements in Bedrock Edition and the Xbox ports. Gameplay is in the first-person perspective by default, but players have the option of a third-person perspective. The game world is composed of rough 3D objects—mainly cubes and fluids, and commonly called blocks —representing various materials, such as dirt, stone, ores, tree trunks (known as \Logs\), water, and lava. The core gameplay revolves around picking up and placing these objects. \n\n ### Game Modes\n - **Survival mode:** Players gather natural resources, craft items, and build structures while managing health and hunger. Hostile mobs spawn at night and in dark areas.\n - **Creative mode:** Players have unlimited resources and the ability to fly, focusing on building and creating without limitations.\n - **Spectator mode:** Players can fly through blocks and spectate other players.\n - **Adventure mode:** Players have restrictions imposed by map creators, emphasizing exploration and puzzle-solving.\n - **Hardcore mode (Java Edition only):** A variant of survival mode with higher difficulty and permadeath.\n\n ### Multiplayer\n *Minecraft* features various multiplayer options, including direct game-to-game multiplayer, LAN play, local split-screen (console-only), and servers (player-hosted and business-hosted). Players can run their own servers, use a hosting provider, or connect directly to another player\s game via Xbox Live. Multiplayer servers have a wide range of activities, with some servers having their own unique rules and customs. The largest and most popular server is Hypixel, which has been visited by over 14 million unique players.\n\n ### Dimensions\n *Minecraft* includes two alternative dimensions besides the Overworld:\n - **The Nether:** A hell-like underworld dimension with unique resources and mobs, accessed via obsidian portals.\n - **The End:** A dimension consisting of floating islands above a void, guarded by the Ender Dragon boss.\n\n ## Customization\n The *Minecraft* modding community has produced a wide variety of downloadable content, including modifications, texture packs, and custom maps. Modifications (mods) range from gameplay changes to entirely new mechanics, while resource packs alter game elements such as textures and sounds. Players can also create and share custom maps with specific rules, challenges, and quests.\n\n ## Legacy and Influence\n *Minecraft* has received critical acclaim and has been cited as one of the greatest video games ever created. It has a massive player base and has been used in educational environments to teach various subjects. Mojang and the *Minecraft* intellectual property were purchased by Microsoft in 2014 for US$2.5 billion. The game has spawned several spin-offs, adaptations, and merchandise, including *Minecraft: Story Mode*, *Minecraft Earth*, *Minecraft Dungeons*, and *Minecraft Legends*. A live-action film adaptation is scheduled for release in 2025.\n'	,
'## Sinopsis\n\n Sumérgete en un mundo sin límites de creatividad y aventura con *Minecraft*, el icónico juego sandbox que permite a los jugadores construir, explorar y sobrevivir en mundos generados proceduralmente de posibilidades infinitas. Ambientado en un universo pixelado y en bloques donde la única limitación es tu imaginación, *Minecraft* ofrece a los jugadores la libertad de dar forma a sus propios destinos mientras extraen recursos, crean herramientas y construyen estructuras elaboradas desde cero. Desde humildes comienzos como un superviviente solitario en un vasto desierto hasta las alturas de ciudades imponentes y civilizaciones expansivas, los jugadores se embarcan en un viaje de descubrimiento y creación como ningún otro. Con sus paisajes infinitos, biomas diversos y oportunidades ilimitadas de exploración y colaboración, *Minecraft* invita a jugadores de todas las edades a liberar su creatividad y embarcarse en aventuras épicas en un mundo limitado solo por su imaginación.\n\n ## Detalles\n\n *Minecraft* es un juego sandbox de 2011 desarrollado por Mojang Studios y lanzado originalmente en 2009. El juego fue creado por Markus Notch Persson en el lenguaje de programación Java. Después de varias versiones de prueba privadas tempranas, se hizo público por primera vez en mayo de 2009 antes de ser lanzado completamente el 18 de noviembre de 2011, con Notch renunciando y Jens Jeb Bergensten asumiendo el desarrollo. *Minecraft* se ha convertido en el videojuego más vendido de la historia, con más de 300 millones de copias vendidas y casi 140 millones de jugadores activos mensuales hasta 2023. Ha sido portado a varias plataformas.\n\n ## Jugabilidad\n\n ### Resumen\n *Minecraft* es un juego sandbox 3D que no tiene objetivos requeridos para cumplir, lo que permite a los jugadores una gran cantidad de libertad para elegir cómo jugar el juego. Sin embargo, existe un sistema de logros, conocido como avances en la Edición Java del juego, trofeos en los puertos de PlayStation y logros en la Edición Bedrock y los puertos de Xbox. La jugabilidad es en la perspectiva de primera persona por defecto, pero los jugadores tienen la opción de una perspectiva de tercera persona. El mundo del juego está compuesto por objetos 3D rugosos, principalmente cubos y fluidos, y comúnmente llamados bloques que representan varios materiales, como tierra, piedra, minerales, troncos de árboles (conocidos como \Troncos\), agua y lava. La jugabilidad principal gira en torno a recoger y colocar estos objetos.\n\n ### Modos de Juego\n - **Modo Supervivencia:** Los jugadores recolectan recursos naturales, crean objetos y construyen estructuras mientras gestionan la salud y el hambre. Los monstruos hostiles aparecen por la noche y en áreas oscuras.\n - **Modo Creativo:** Los jugadores tienen recursos ilimitados y la capacidad de volar, centrándose en construir y crear sin limitaciones.\n - **Modo Espectador:** Los jugadores pueden volar a través de bloques y ver a otros jugadores.\n - **Modo Aventura:** Los jugadores tienen restricciones impuestas por los creadores de mapas, enfatizando la exploración y la resolución de acertijos.\n - **Modo Difícil (solo Edición Java):** Una variante del modo supervivencia con mayor dificultad y muerte permanente.\n\n ### Multijugador\n *Minecraft* cuenta con varias opciones multijugador, incluyendo multijugador directo de juego a juego, juego en LAN, pantalla dividida local (solo consola) y servidores (jugador alojados y de negocios). Los jugadores pueden ejecutar sus propios servidores, usar un proveedor de alojamiento o conectarse directamente al juego de otro jugador a través de Xbox Live. Los servidores multijugador tienen una amplia gama de actividades, con algunos servidores que tienen sus propias reglas y costumbres únicas. El servidor más grande y popular es Hypixel, que ha sido visitado por más de 14 millones de jugadores únicos.\n\n ### Dimensiones\n *Minecraft* incluye dos dimensiones alternativas además del Overworld:\n - **El Nether:** Una dimensión similar al infierno con recursos y monstruos únicos, a la que se accede a través de portales de obsidiana.\n - **El Fin:** Una dimensión que consiste en islas flotantes sobre un vacío, custodiada por el jefe Ender Dragon.\n\n ## Personalización\n La comunidad de modificación de *Minecraft* ha producido una amplia variedad de contenido descargable, incluidas modificaciones, paquetes de texturas y mapas personalizados. Las modificaciones (mods) van desde cambios en la jugabilidad hasta mecánicas completamente nuevas, mientras que los paquetes de recursos alteran elementos del juego como texturas y sonidos. Los jugadores también pueden crear y compartir mapas personalizados con reglas específicas, desafíos y misiones.\n\n ## Legado e Influencia\n *Minecraft* ha recibido elogios de la crítica y ha sido citado como uno de los mejores videojuegos jamás creados. Tiene una base de jugadores masiva y se ha utilizado en entornos educativos para enseñar diversas materias. Mojang y la propiedad intelectual de *Minecraft* fueron compradas por Microsoft en 2014 por US$2.5 mil millones. El juego ha generado varios spin-offs, adaptaciones y mercancías, incluyendo *Minecraft: Story Mode*, *Minecraft Earth*, *Minecraft Dungeons* y *Minecraft Legends*. Una adaptación cinematográfica de acción en vivo está programada para ser lanzada en 2025.\n',

'## Synopsis\n\n Embark on a grand odyssey through ancient Greece in *Assassin\s Creed Odyssey*, an epic action-adventure game that immerses players in a rich and vibrant world of myth, legend, and intrigue. Set in the midst of the Peloponnesian War, players assume the role of either Alexios or Kassandra, a mercenary of Spartan descent, as they uncover the truth behind their mysterious lineage and unravel the secrets of their destiny. With its sprawling open-world environment, players traverse the sun-drenched islands and bustling cities of ancient Greece, encountering legendary figures from history and myth as they shape the course of history. From epic naval battles and stealthy assassinations to thrilling skirmishes and epic quests, *Assassin\s Creed Odyssey* offers a diverse and immersive gameplay experience that caters to a wide range of playstyles. With its breathtaking visuals, compelling narrative, and vast array of activities and side quests, *Assassin\s Creed Odyssey* invites players to embark on an unforgettable journey through one of history\s most captivating periods.\n\n ## Development and Release\n\n *Assassin\s Creed Odyssey* is a 2018 action role-playing video game developed by Ubisoft Quebec and published by Ubisoft. It is the eleventh major installment in the *Assassin\s Creed* series and the successor to 2017\s *Assassin\s Creed Origins*. Like its predecessor, the game features a large open world and adopts many elements from the role-playing genre, putting more emphasis on combat and exploration than stealth. Naval combat from previous titles in the series also plays a prominent role in *Odyssey*. The game\s plot tells a mythological history of the Peloponnesian War between Athens and Sparta from 431 to 422 BC.\n\n ## Gameplay\n\n In *Odyssey*, players can participate in conquest battles and fight for either the Athenians or the Spartans. The game is played from a third-person perspective, and players can select to play as either Alexios or Kassandra, Greek mercenaries and descendants of the Spartan king Leonidas I. In addition to completing the story campaign, players can freely explore a large open world set in Greece on foot or on horseback. They can encounter various non-playable characters (NPCs) who give players side missions to complete and discover locations of interests, clear out fortresses and camps, explore tombs and shipwrecks, and collect hidden treasures. The game offers two modes of gameplay: Guided mode shows the player the locations of their objects immediately using waypoints, while Exploration mode tasks players to find out the locations themselves after being given brief clues from other NPCs.\n\n Combat in *Odyssey* features two modes of melee attack—light attacks are fast but weak, while heavy attacks are slow but strong. Players can also dodge hostile attacks or parry them. The player character can use different types of melee weapons such as spears, heavy blunt weapons, daggers, swords, and bows and arrows to defeat enemies. The game features a weapon and gear system in which each weapon and piece of armour the player wears has different statistics and provides a range of advantages. Players can also commandeer a warship named Adrestia to explore the Aegean Sea, engage in naval combat, and board enemy ships.\n\n ## Plot and Characters\n\n As with previous games in the series, *Odyssey* features a narrative set in the modern-day, following Layla Hassan, an Assassin and former Abstergo researcher who was introduced in *Origins*. Assisted by fellow Assassins, Layla\s goal is to find the Staff of Hermes Trismegistus and the lost city of Atlantis by using data processed by her portable Animus device. The historical plot is set in 431-422 BC, four centuries before the events of *Origins* and the creation of the Hidden Ones, the forerunners to the Brotherhood of Assassins.\n\n The game\s main storyline follows the player character, known as the Eagle Bearer, a legendary mercenary with a mysterious lineage. As the Eagle Bearer, players navigate through the political intrigues and conflicts of ancient Greece, confronting the Cult of Kosmos, a secret organization bent on manipulating the course of history. Along the way, players encounter historical and mythical figures, including Alkibiades, Aristophanes, Euripides, Democritus, and Sokrates, as well as creatures from Greek mythology such as Medusa, the Cyclops, the Sphinx, and the Minotaur.\n\n ## Expansions\n\n *Assassin\s Creed Odyssey* received several expansions, including *Legacy of the First Blade* and *The Fate of Atlantis*. These expansions further explore the lore and mythology of ancient Greece, introducing new characters and storylines that expand upon the main game\s narrative.\n\n ## Reception and Legacy\n\n *Assassin\s Creed Odyssey* received generally positive reviews from critics, with praise for its gameplay, graphics, characters, role-playing elements, and world design. However, it was criticized for its overambitiousness, pacing, and the inclusion of microtransactions. Despite these criticisms, *Odyssey* was a commercial success, selling over 10 million copies worldwide by March 2020. The game\s success paved the way for *Assassin\s Creed Valhalla*, which was released in November 2020, continuing the series\ exploration of historical settings and narratives.\n\n'	,

La trama histórica está ambientada en el 431-422 a.C., cuatro siglos antes de los eventos de *Origins* y la creación de los Ocultos, los precursores de la Hermandad de los Asesinos.\n\n La historia principal del juego sigue al personaje del jugador, conocido como el Portador del Águila, un mercenario legendario con un linaje misterioso. Their journey leads them to the town of Folsense, where they uncover the truth behind the box\s legend and the town\s dark past. '## Sinopsis\n\n *El profesor Layton y la caja de Pandora*, conocido como *Professor Layton and Pandora\s Box* en Australia y Europa, es la segunda entrega en la serie del profesor Layton desarrollada por Level-5. El juego sigue al Profesor Layton y su aprendiz Luke mientras se embarcan en un viaje en tren para desentrañar el misterio que rodea a una caja mortal de la que se rumorea que mata a cualquiera que la abra.\n\n ## Jugabilidad\n\n *El profesor Layton y la caja de Pandora* es un juego de aventura/puzles en el que los jugadores controlan al Profesor Layton y a Luke mientras recorren diversas ubicaciones. Además de resolver una variedad de puzles, los jugadores deben explorar diferentes áreas, resolver misterios y ayudar al Profesor en su búsqueda. Los puzles van desde acertijos hasta rompecabezas lógicos, y los jugadores ganan picarats por cada solución correcta. El juego cuenta con monedas de pista para ayudar a los jugadores a resolver puzles, y completarlos recompensa a los jugadores con varios objetos y recompensas.\n\n ## Personajes\n\n - Profesor Layton: el protagonista titular y un arqueólogo renombrado por resolver puzles.\n - Luke: el autoproclamado aprendiz de Layton que lo acompaña en sus aventuras.\n - Flora: una joven que se une a Layton y Luke en su viaje.\n - Inspector Chelmey: un detective que persigue el misterio que rodea a la Caja Diabólica.\n - Don Paolo: el archirrival de Layton que juega un papel importante en los eventos del juego.\n - Dr. Schrader: el mentor de Layton que se involucra en el misterio de la caja de Pandora.\n\n ## Argumento\n\n El juego comienza con Layton y Luke investigando la desaparición del Dr. Schrader y el robo de la caja de Pandora. Su viaje los lleva a la ciudad de Folsense, donde descubren la verdad detrás de la leyenda de la caja y el oscuro pasado de la ciudad. En el camino, se encuentran con varios personajes, incluyendo sospechosos y aliados, mientras desentrañan el misterio.\n\n ## Desarrollo\n\n El juego estaba originalmente planeado para llamarse *Layton-kyōju to Yū-rei Jima no Himitsu* (Professor Layton y el Secreto de la Isla Fantasma) pero se cambió a *la caja de Pandora* debido a cuestiones sobre la trama. Level-5 tenía como objetivo integrar los puzles de manera más fluida en la narrativa del juego después de recibir comentarios del primer juego de la serie. También se enfocaron en actualizar los sistemas de juego existentes y aumentar el tamaño de los datos del juego.\n'	,

('Professor Layton and the Unwound Future',	'El profesor Layton y el futuro perdido',	2010	,'https://www.guiasnintendo.com/0_NINTENDO_DS/profesor_layton_futuro_perdido/profesor_layton_futuro_perdido_sp/welcome.html',	
'## Synopsis\n\n *Professor Layton and the Unwound Future*, known as *Professor Layton and the Lost Future* in Europe and Australia, is the third game in the first trilogy of the Professor Layton puzzle game series by Level-5. It was first released in Japan in November 2008 and was later released in North America in September 2010 and in Europe and Australia in October 2010. In the game, Layton meets an older version of his apprentice, Luke, who brings him to a terrible future he wishes him to help fix. The game received critical acclaim by critics, praise for its story, puzzles, characters, soundtrack, and has since been cited as one of the best games of the series. An enhanced mobile port of Unwound Future, subtitled HD for Mobile was released on July 13, 2020.\n\n ## Gameplay\n\n As with previous Professor Layton games, Unwound Future is an adventure game where the player solves puzzles offered by local citizens to progress the story forward, through dialogue and around 32 minutes of full motion video. The player moves about the game through still images of locations. The player can use the DS touchscreen to tap on non-player characters to start a dialog or to obtain a puzzle, and also can search anywhere on the background for hint coins, with some areas needing to be tapped several times to reveal a secret hint coin or puzzle. Puzzles are brainteasers of many varieties, including visual, math, and logic. There is no time limit to solve puzzles, and the player can get up to 3 hints at a cost of one hint coin each, a new feature in Unwound Future is a super hint costing 2 coins, that can only be bought after the other 3 hints have been revealed, but that nearly reveals the puzzle\s solution. If the player is correct in solving the puzzle, they gain a number of Picarats a form of currency within the game. Guessing the incorrect answer will reduce the number of picarats the player can get on subsequent attempts. Players can visit certain areas in order to play undiscovered or unsolved puzzles that are left behind as the story progresses.\n\n As part of rewards for solving puzzles, the player may play one of three mini-games that support additional puzzles in Layton\s Trunk that can be attempted at any time. One mini-game is based on sticker books, placing the correct stickers at locations in the book to make the story make sense. Another requires training a parrot to carry items to a character using a series of ropes to act as perches or rebounding walls. The third mini-game is a toy car that the player must drive across specific tiles on a map using a series of directional indicators. Layton\s Bag also contains details on the story, characters, and a list of completed puzzles the player can review and try again.\n\n After completing the game, several other puzzle challenges become available in the game\s bonus features, many more difficult than the main game puzzles. When the player has completed all the puzzles within the game, a final puzzle is revealed. Players may also access a number of bonus features depending on how many picarats they have accumulated throughout the game.\n\n As with the previous two titles in the series, additional weekly puzzles were available for download via the Bonus menu, with one being released each week from the original release date, for 30 weeks. After May 20, 2014, it\s no longer possible to download the additional content, as the Nintendo Wi-Fi Connection service was terminated on that date.\n\n ## Plot\n\n As Layton and Luke are invited to witness a demonstration of a time machine built by Dr. Alain Stahngun, the experiment goes awry, causing the disappearance of Stahngun and the prime minister, Bill Hawks. One week later, as numerous scientists have been reported missing, Layton and Luke receive a letter purporting to be from Luke ten years in the future, leading the two to a quaint clock shop in the London back alleys. Inside, the old couple who own the shop show the two another time machine in the guise of a giant clock, and the pair find themselves in a drastically-changed quasi-steam punk London ten years from their present, where they meet the Future Luke. He explains that in this future, Layton has become the head of a mafia-like mob known as the Family and taken control of London. Layton and Luke agree to assist Future Luke in stopping this Future Layton. After briefly returning to the past to look up some files pertaining to an accident which claimed the life of his girlfriend, Claire, ten years ago, Layton and Luke return to the future London, inadvertently bringing Flora, Inspector Chelmey and his assistant Barton with him. As the group investigates the whereabouts of Future Layton, Luke becomes withdrawn for a short time. It\s revealed that his family is moving overseas, and he\s afraid of losing his friendship with Layton. Layton reassures him that their friendship will persist even when they\re apart, and they resume the investigation.\n\n Travelling through Chinatown and up a giant pagoda, the group encounter Future Layton, where he is revealed to be Dr. Stahngun, whose true identity is Dimitri Allen. He reveals to have taken Bill hostage, and wants to build the time machine to save Claire from the accident that happened 10 years prior to Layton\s present time. This led to Dimitri\s dedication to build a working time machine and return to the past so he can save Claire\s life. He also used Layton\s identity to not only hide its own, but also tease the real Layton to come to him so he can obtain Layton\s memories in order to create the bridge in space-time so he could reach the moment of the explosion to save Claire. Dimitri attempts to trap Layton, but this plan is foiled when Don Paolo, a recurring villain-turned-hero of the series, reveals that he has been disguised as Layton to help and that he also loved Claire.\n\n Together they infiltrate Dimitri\s base of operations to free the other scientists, where Layton encounters Claire\s near-identical sister, Celeste, who assists them in escaping. As everyone gathers at the Thames Arms restaurant, where Dimitri is also waiting for them disguised as the bartender, Layton manages to deduce that they are not actually in the future, but in a pseudo-replica of London built in a cavern. The purpose of this replica was to fool the scientists into thinking they were stranded 10 years from home, motivating them to build a time machine in order to return home. Dimitri built this replica London when he realized that he alone could not construct a working time machine and needed scientists that were just as motivated as him. He reveals that Bill and him, along with Claire (whom he also had feelings for), were working on a time machine ten years ago, but Bill\s desire for money made him sell a crucial part, which led to the accident that claimed Claire\s life. This led to Dimitri\s dedication to build a working time machine and return to the past so he can save Claire\s life. Layton also deduces that Dimitri is but a pawn compared to the true mastermind, Future Luke, whose true identity is Clive, a boy who sought revenge against Dimitri, Bill and London in general as the explosion that killed Claire also took his parents away from him.\n\n Kidnapping Flora, Clive escapes to his mobile fortress, the machine the scientists had really been working on without Dimitri\s knowledge, which he brings to the surface to attack London. With help from Don Paolo, Layton and Luke manage to board the fortress and free Flora, later joined by Celeste. After deducing that they need to reverse the flow of power from the generator, they discover Bill is attached to the generator, wired to a bomb. With thanks to Celeste\s old watch, they manage to reroute the bomb\s wires, free Bill and reverse the power flow of the fortress, causing it to collapse. After flying Don Paolo\s modified Laytonmobile to get everyone to the ground, where Chelmey manages to evacuate the underground citizens, Layton returns to help Celeste rescue Clive from the fortress before it falls down into the fake future London and explodes.\n\n As everyone safely regroups, Clive is put under arrest but promises to atone for his crimes, thanking Layton for comforting him as he did the day his parents were killed. It is then revealed that Celeste is actually Claire herself, who was teleported ten years into the future during the accident. However, her presence had become unstable and would soon send her back in time to the moment of her death, leading Dimitri to try to find a way to save her but to no avail. Accepting her fate, Claire has a tearful final reunion with Layton before bidding farewell and disappearing back to her time, to the moment of her death. Layton, although crushed to lose Claire again, finally comes to terms with his loss and removes his hat out of respect to her as it snows.\n\n After the incident, Layton bids farewell to Luke as he boards a ship to his new home. Some time later, Layton receives a letter from Luke, inviting him to investigate another puzzling situation with him, in Steam Bison, America.\n\n ## Release\n\n The game was released in Japan on November 27, 2008, and was the 15th best-selling game in 2008. A western localization of the game was revealed at E3 2010, with a September 20, 2010 release date for North America, and an October 22, 2010 release date for Europe. At the same time in the UK, an English localization of the film *Professor Layton and the Eternal Diva* was released. An English trailer was also shown. The North American release date was later pushed to September 12, 2010.\n\n ## Music\n\n Like the previous two games, the game\s music was composed by Tomohito Nishiura and later released in Japan, on an album titled *Layton Kyoju to Saigo no Jikan Ryoko Original Soundtrack*. Several entirely new puzzle themes were composed for puzzles in this game. *Unwound Future*\s ending theme, Time Travel\ was sung by Ann Sally in the original Japanese versions, while the international versions replaced it with an instrumental version. The soundtrack album replaces the vocal theme with a separate piano version, not included in either release of the game.\n'	,
'## Sinopsis\n\n *El profesor Layton y el futuro perdido*, conocido como *Professor Layton and the Lost Future* en Europa y Australia, es el tercer juego en la primera trilogía de la serie de juegos de rompecabezas Professor Layton desarrollada por Level-5. Fue lanzado por primera vez en Japón en noviembre de 2008 y más tarde en América del Norte en septiembre de 2010 y en Europa y Australia en octubre de 2010. En el juego, Layton conoce a una versión mayor de su aprendiz, Luke, quien lo lleva a un terrible futuro que él desea ayudar a arreglar. El juego recibió elogios de la crítica por su historia, puzles, personajes, banda sonora, y desde entonces ha sido citado como uno de los mejores juegos de la serie. Una versión mejorada para móviles de *Unwound Future*, subtitulada HD for Mobile fue lanzada el 13 de julio de 2020.\n\n ## Jugabilidad\n\n Al igual que con los juegos anteriores del profesor Layton, el Futuro Perdido es un juego de aventuras en el que el jugador resuelve puzles ofrecidos por los ciudadanos locales para avanzar en la historia, a través de diálogos y alrededor de 32 minutos de video en movimiento completo. El jugador se mueve por el juego a través de imágenes fijas de ubicaciones. El jugador puede usar la pantalla táctil de la DS para tocar a los personajes no jugadores y comenzar un diálogo o para obtener un puzle, y también puede buscar en cualquier lugar del fondo en busca de monedas de pista, con algunas áreas que deben tocarse varias veces para revelar una moneda de pista secreta o un puzle. Los puzles son acertijos de muchas variedades, incluyendo visuales, matemáticos y lógicos. No hay límite de tiempo para resolver los puzles, y el jugador puede obtener hasta 3 pistas a cambio de una moneda de pista cada una. Una nueva función en esta entrega de la saga es una pista especial que cuesta 2 monedas, que solo se puede comprar después de que se hayan revelado las otras 3 pistas, pero que revela casi completamente la solución del puzle. Si el jugador resuelve correctamente el puzle, gana un número de Picarats una forma de moneda dentro del juego. Introducir una respuesta incorrecta reducirá el número de picarats que el jugador puede obtener en intentos posteriores. Los jugadores pueden visitar ciertas áreas para jugar puzles no descubiertos o sin resolver que se quedan atrás a medida que avanza la historia.\n\n Como parte de las recompensas por resolver puzles, el jugador puede jugar uno de tres mini-juegos que admiten puzles adicionales en el Baúl de Layton que se pueden intentar en cualquier momento. Uno de los mini-juegos se basa en libros de pegatinas, colocando las pegatinas correctas en ubicaciones en el libro para que la historia tenga sentido. Otro requiere entrenar a un loro para llevar objetos a un personaje usando una serie de cuerdas para actuar como perchas o paredes de rebote. El tercer mini-juego es un coche de juguete que el jugador debe conducir sobre casillas específicas en un mapa usando una serie de indicadores direccionales. La Bolsa de Layton también contiene detalles sobre la historia, los personajes y una lista de puzles completados que el jugador puede revisar y volver a intentar.\n\n Después de completar el juego, varios desafíos de puzles adicionales están disponibles en las características de bonificación del juego, muchos más difíciles que los puzles del juego principal. Cuando el jugador ha completado todos los puzles dentro del juego, se revela un puzle final. Los jugadores también pueden acceder a varias características de bonificación dependiendo de cuántos picarats hayan acumulado a lo largo del juego.\n\n Al igual que en los dos títulos anteriores de la serie, se podían descargar puzles semanales adicionales a través del menú de bonificación, con uno siendo lanzado cada semana desde la fecha de lanzamiento original, durante 30 semanas. Después del 20 de mayo de 2014, ya no es posible descargar el contenido adicional, ya que el servicio de Conexión Wi-Fi de Nintendo fue clausurado en esa fecha.\n\n ## Trama\n\n Cuando Layton y Luke son invitados a presenciar una demostración de una máquina del tiempo construida por el Dr. Alain Stahngun, el experimento sale mal, causando la desaparición de Stahngun y el primer ministro, Bill Hawks. Una semana después, cuando se ha informado de la desaparición de numerosos científicos, Layton y Luke reciben una carta que supuestamente es de Luke diez años en el futuro, lo que lleva a los dos a una pintoresca tienda de relojes en los callejones traseros de Londres. Dentro, la pareja de ancianos que posee la tienda muestra a los dos otra máquina del tiempo disfrazada de un reloj gigante, y la pareja se encuentra en un Londres pseudo-steampunk drásticamente cambiado diez años desde su presente, donde conocen al Luke del futuro. Él explica que en este futuro, Layton se ha convertido en el jefe de una mafia conocida como la Familia y ha tomado el control de Londres. Layton y Luke acuerdan ayudar al Luke del futuro a detener a este nuevo Layton. Después de regresar brevemente al pasado para buscar algunos archivos relacionados con un accidente que se cobró la vida de su novia, Claire, hace diez años, Layton y Luke regresan al Londres del futuro, llevando inadvertidamente a Flora, el inspector Chelmey y su asistente Barton con ellos. Mientras el grupo investiga el paradero del Futuro Layton, Luke se retira brevemente durante un corto tiempo. Se revela que su familia se está mudando al extranjero, y teme perder su amistad con Layton. Layton lo tranquiliza diciendo que su amistad persistirá incluso cuando estén separados, y reanudan la investigación.\n\n Viajando a través de Chinatown y subiendo una pagoda gigante, el grupo se encuentra con el Layton del futuro, donde se revela que es el Dr. Stahngun, cuya verdadera identidad es Dimitri Allen. Revela haber tomado como rehén a Bill, y quiere construir la máquina del tiempo para salvar a Claire del accidente que ocurrió 10 años antes del tiempo presente de Layton. Esto llevó a la dedicación de Dimitri para construir una máquina del tiempo funcional y regresar al pasado para poder salvar la vida de Claire. También usó la identidad de Layton no solo para ocultar la suya, sino también para burlarse del verdadero Layton para que vaya hacia él para que pueda obtener los recuerdos de Layton para crear el puente en el espacio-tiempo para que pudiera llegar al momento de la explosión para salvar a Claire. Dimitri intenta atrapar a Layton, pero este plan es frustrado cuando Don Paolo, un villano recurrente convertido en héroe de la serie, revela que ha estado disfrazado de Layton para ayudar y que también amaba a Claire.\n\n Juntos infiltran la base de operaciones de Dimitri para liberar a los otros científicos, donde Layton se encuentra con la hermana casi idéntica de Claire, Celeste, quien los ayuda a escapar. Mientras todos se reúnen en el restaurante Thames Arms, donde Dimitri también los espera disfrazado de camarero, Layton logra deducir que en realidad no están en el futuro, sino en una réplica pseudo de Londres construida en una caverna. El propósito de esta réplica era engañar a los científicos para que creyeran que estaban varados 10 años lejos de casa, motivándolos a construir una máquina del tiempo para regresar a casa. Dimitri construyó esta réplica de Londres cuando se dio cuenta de que él solo no podía construir una máquina del tiempo funcional y necesitaba científicos que estuvieran tan motivados como él. Revela que él y Bill, junto con Claire (de quien también tenía sentimientos), estaban trabajando en una máquina del tiempo hace diez años, pero el deseo de dinero de Bill lo llevó a vender una parte crucial, lo que llevó al accidente que se cobró la vida de Claire. Esto llevó a la dedicación de Dimitri para construir una máquina del tiempo funcional y regresar al pasado para poder salvar la vida de Claire. Layton también deduce que Dimitri es solo un peón en comparación con el verdadero cerebro detrás de todo, el Futuro Luke, cuya verdadera identidad es Clive, un niño que buscaba venganza contra Dimitri, Bill y Londres en general, ya que la explosión que mató a Claire también se llevó a sus padres.\n\n Secuestrando a Flora, Clive escapa a su fortaleza móvil, la máquina en la que los científicos realmente habían estado trabajando sin el conocimiento de Dimitri, que lleva a la superficie para atacar a Londres. Con la ayuda de Don Paolo, Layton y Luke logran abordar la fortaleza y liberar a Flora, a quien luego se une Celeste. Después de deducir que necesitan revertir el flujo de energía del generador, descubren que Bill está conectado al generador, conectado a una bomba. Gracias al viejo reloj de Celeste, logran redirigir los cables de la bomba, liberar a Bill y revertir el flujo de energía de la fortaleza, lo que hace que colapse. Después de volar en el Laytonmóvil modificado de Don Paolo para llevar a todos al suelo, donde Chelmey logra evacuar a los ciudadanos del subterráneo, Layton regresa para ayudar a Celeste a rescatar a Clive de la fortaleza antes de que caiga en el falso futuro de Londres y explote.\n\n Cuando todos se reúnen de manera segura, Clive es arrestado pero promete expiar sus crímenes, agradeciéndole a Layton por reconfortarlo como lo hizo el día que sus padres fueron asesinados. Luego se revela que Celeste es en realidad Claire misma, quien fue teletransportada diez años al futuro durante el accidente. Sin embargo, su presencia se había vuelto inestable y pronto la enviaría de regreso en el tiempo al momento de su muerte, lo que llevó a Dimitri a intentar encontrar una manera de salvarla, pero sin éxito. Aceptando su destino, Claire tiene una emotiva reunión final con Layton antes de despedirse y desaparecer de regreso a su tiempo, al momento de su muerte. Layton, aunque destrozado por perder a Claire nuevamente, finalmente acepta su pérdida y se quita el sombrero en señal de respeto hacia ella mientras nieva.\n\n Después del incidente, Layton se despide de Luke mientras aborda un barco hacia su nuevo hogar. Algún tiempo después, Layton recibe una carta de Luke, invitándolo a investigar otra situación desconcertante con él, en Steam Bison, América.\n\n ## Lanzamiento\n\n El juego fue lanzado en Japón el 27 de noviembre de 2008, y fue el 15º juego más vendido en 2008. Una localización occidental del juego fue revelada en el E3 2010, con una fecha de lanzamiento del 20 de septiembre de 2010 para América del Norte y el 22 de octubre de 2010 para Europa. Al mismo tiempo en el Reino Unido, se lanzó una localización en inglés de la película *Professor Layton and the Eternal Diva*. También se mostró un tráiler en inglés. La fecha de lanzamiento en América del Norte se retrasó posteriormente al 12 de septiembre de 2010.\n\n ## Música\n\n Al igual que los dos juegos anteriores, la música del juego fue compuesta por Tomohito Nishiura y luego lanzada en Japón, en un álbum titulado *Layton Kyoju to Saigo no Jikan Ryoko Original Soundtrack*. Se compusieron varios temas de puzles completamente nuevos para los puzles de este juego. El tema de cierre de *Unwound Future*, Time Travel\ fue cantado por Ann Sally en las versiones japonesas originales, mientras que las versiones internacionales lo reemplazaron con una versión instrumental. El álbum de la banda sonora reemplaza el tema vocal con una versión de piano separada, que no está incluida en ninguna de las versiones del juego.\n'	,
